\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    % Nicer default font (+ math font) than Computer Modern for most use cases
    \usepackage{mathpazo}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }

    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document

    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)

\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}

\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%

    \hypertarget{try-16-setup-paprika-restraints}{%
\section{\texorpdfstring{Try 16: setup \texttt{paprika}
restraints}{Try 16: setup paprika restraints}}\label{try-16-setup-paprika-restraints}}

    Presuming we have a host-guest system already setup, let's see if we can
rationally instruct \texttt{paprika} to setup all the restraints for a
real system.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}1}]:} \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{k}{load\PYZus{}ext} autoreload
        \PY{o}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{k}{autoreload} 2
        
        \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{os} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{os}
        \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{numpy} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{np}
        
        \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{parmed} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{pmd}
        \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{pytraj} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{pt}
\end{Verbatim}

        \PY{n}{logging}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{info}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Started logging...}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{paprika}

    \hypertarget{preamble}{%
\subsection{Preamble}\label{preamble}}

    We are going to setup host translational restraints, guest translational
restraints, host ``jacks,'' and guest wall restraints with
\texttt{paprika}. First, let's try working in a directory where we have
a known \texttt{disang.rest} file we can use as a reference:
\texttt{/data/davids4/projects/smirnoff-host-guest/a-bam-p/a00/original}
or
\texttt{/data/davids4/projects/smirnoff-host-guest/a-bam-p/u00/original}
for the final values.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}3}]:} \PY{n}{dummy\PYZus{}anchors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{:8}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{:9}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{:10}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{host\PYZus{}anchors}  \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{:1@O3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{:3@C1}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{:5@C6}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{guest\PYZus{}anchors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{:7@C4}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{:7@N1}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}4}]:} \PY{n}{hg} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pmd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load\PYZus{}file}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{systems/a\PYZhy{}bam\PYZhy{}p/smirnoff/a000/smirnoff.prmtop}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                           \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{systems/a\PYZhy{}bam\PYZhy{}p/smirnoff/a000/smirnoff.inpcrd}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                            \PY{n}{structure}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


    The attach fractions can be found in the \texttt{Setup.pl} file in the
original location on \texttt{kirkwood}:
\texttt{/data/nhenriksen/projects/cds/wat6/bgbg-tip3p/a-bam-p/a00/}
under \texttt{@AttachFC}.

    The attach force constant is 5.0 kcal/mol-A\^{}\{2\} for distances and
100.0 kcal/mol-rad\^{}\{2\} for angels and torsions based on
\texttt{disang.rest} in \texttt{u00}.

    The pull distances are specified by \texttt{@Translate} in
\texttt{Setup.pl} and are offset by 6 Angstroms.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}5}]:} \PY{n}{attach\PYZus{}string} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{0.00 0.40 0.80 1.60 2.40 4.00 5.50 8.65 11.80 18.10 24.40 37.00 49.60 74.80 100.00}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
        \PY{n}{attach\PYZus{}fractions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{100} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{attach\PYZus{}string}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}
        
        \PY{n}{pull\PYZus{}string} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{0.00 0.40 0.80 1.20 1.60 2.00 2.40 2.80 3.20 3.60 4.00 4.40 4.80 5.20 5.60 6.00 6.40 6.80 7.20 7.60 8.00 8.40 8.80 9.20 9.60 10.00 10.40 10.80 11.20 11.60 12.00 12.40 12.80 13.20 13.60 14.00 14.40 14.80 15.20 15.60 16.00 16.40 16.80 17.20 17.60 18.00}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
        \PY{n}{pull\PYZus{}distances} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n+nb}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mf}{6.00} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{pull\PYZus{}string}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{split}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}
        
        \PY{n}{windows} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{attach\PYZus{}fractions}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pull\PYZus{}distances}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{f}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{There are }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}windows\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ windows in this attach\PYZhy{}pull calculation.}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

There are [15, 46, 0] windows in this attach-pull calculation.

    \hypertarget{define-the-host-translational-restraints}{%
\subsection{Define the host translational
restraints}\label{define-the-host-translational-restraints}}

These restraints help pin down the host during initial attachment of the
DAT restraints. They are static, meaning unlike other restraints, they
are not turned on slowly during the attachment phase.

and C1\_n - O1\_n - C4\_n+1 - C5\_n+1.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

                                       \PY{p}{]}

\end{Verbatim}


    \hypertarget{define-the-guest-wall-restraints}{%
\subsection{Define the guest ``wall''
restraints}\label{define-the-guest-wall-restraints}}

    The guest wall restraints are only on during the attachment phase, and
make sure that the guest does not unbind and waste time diffusing around
the simulation box. These distance restraints are flat from zero through
the restraint target value, near the edge of the binding cavity, and
then increase harmonically beyond that. The guest ``wall'' angle
restraint is harmonic and prevents the guest from flipping around during
the bound phase.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}9}]:} \PY{n}{guest\PYZus{}wall\PYZus{}template} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}
            \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{O2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{guest\PYZus{}anchors}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{O6}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{guest\PYZus{}anchors}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{p}{]}
        
        \PY{n}{guest\PYZus{}wall\PYZus{}restraint\PYZus{}atoms} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{guest\PYZus{}wall\PYZus{}restraint\PYZus{}targets} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{guest\PYZus{}wall\PYZus{}restraint\PYZus{}angle\PYZus{}fc} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{500.0}
        \PY{n}{guest\PYZus{}wall\PYZus{}restraint\PYZus{}distance\PYZus{}fc} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{50.0}
        
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{n} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{first\PYZus{}host\PYZus{}residue}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{host\PYZus{}residues} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{first\PYZus{}host\PYZus{}residue}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{guest\PYZus{}wall\PYZus{}restraint\PYZus{}atoms}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}
                \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{f}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{:}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}n\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{@}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}guest\PYZus{}wall\PYZus{}template[0][0]\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                 \PY{n}{f}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}guest\PYZus{}wall\PYZus{}template[0][1]\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                \PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
